                <script type="text/javascript">
        function submitDeliverySelectionForm() {
            var selectedStore = '';
            var selectedAddress = '';
            var selectedShippingMethod = '';
            var selectedPickingCenter = '';
            var page = ''; 
            
            if (selectedStore !== '') {
                submitSelectedStoreForm(selectedStore, selectedPickingCenter,page);
            } else if (selectedAddress !== '') {
                submitSelectAddressForm(selectedAddress, selectedPickingCenter,page);
            } else if (selectedShippingMethod !== '') {
                submitSelectShippingMethodForm(selectedShippingMethod, selectedPickingCenter,page);
            } else {
                //TODO alert user about invalid selection
            }
        }
        function closeModalPopup(modalId) {
        	var elem = document.getElementById(modalId);
        	elem.style.display="none";
        	var elem1 = document.getElementsByClassName('modal-backdrop fade in');
          	document.body.removeChild(elem1[0]);
          	if($("#currentSiteId").val() == $("#chileSiteId").val()){
     		   $.ajax({
     	           type:"post",
     	           dataType:"html",
     	           url:contextroot+"/myaccount/gadgets/saveOrRevertShippingMethod.jsp",
     	           data: {
     	               state : "revert"
     	           },
     	           success: function(data){
     					console.log("Reverted previous shipping method");
     	           },
     	           error: function (xhr, status) {
     	            alert('Disculpe, existi� un problema');
     	           }
     	       });
     	   }
        	window.location.href=window.location.href;
        }
    </script>

$(document).ready(function(){
      // galeria
      function fp_gallery_img(){

        var url_l = window.location.href,
            url_short = window.location.href.split("/"),

                  .after('&lt;iframe class="fp_target_video" style="width:100%;height:280px;" class="fp_video_iframe" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/'+ fp_video_id +'?autoplay=0&amp;rel=0" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;');
                }else{
                  $(".fp-gallery-img-active").show();
                  if( $(".fp_target_video").length &amp;&amp; $(".fp_target_video").is(":visible") ){
                    $(".fp_target_video").hide();
                  }
                }
                $(".fp-gallery-thumbnails").find("img").parent("div").removeClass("fp-img-active");
                _this.parent("div").addClass("fp-img-active");
                $(".fp-gallery-img-active").attr("src", src);                
              })
            }
          }
        }
      }
      fp_gallery_img();
  })

<script type="text/javascript">
  $("nav.supermenu &gt; ul &gt; li").bind('tap mouseover', function(e) { // binding onclick
          if ($(this).hasClass('selected')) {
          } else {
            $("nav.supermenu &gt; ul &gt;.selected &gt; ul").slideUp(1); // hiding popups
            $("nav.supermenu &gt; ul &gt;.selected").removeClass("selected");
            if ($(this).children('ul').length) {
              $(this).addClass("selected"); // display popup
              $(this).children('ul').slideDown(1);
            }
          }
          e.stopPropagation();
        }); 
        $(".sm-supermercado &gt; ul &gt; li").bind('tap mouseover', function(e) { // binding onclick
          if ($(this).hasClass('selectedsub')) {
          } else {
            $(".sm-supermercado &gt; ul &gt; .selectedsub &gt; ul").slideUp(1); // hiding popups
            $(".sm-supermercado &gt; ul &gt; .selectedsub").removeClass("selectedsub");
            if ($(this).children('ul').length) {
              $(this).addClass("selectedsub"); // display popup
              $(this).children('ul').slideDown(1);
            }
          }
          e.stopPropagation();
        }); 
          $("body").bind('tap mouseover', function(e) { // binding onclick to body

          $("nav.supermenu &gt; ul &gt; .selected &gt; ul").fadeOut(500); // hiding popups        
          $("nav.supermenu &gt; ul &gt; .selected").removeClass("selected");  
          $(".sm-supermercado &gt; ul &gt; .selectedsub &gt; ul").fadeOut(500); // hiding popups        
          $(".sm-supermercado &gt; ul &gt; .selectedsub").removeClass("selectedsub");       
          e.stopPropagation();/*
          var myVar;
        myVar = setTimeout(desvanecer, 1000);*/
        }); 
    
 
    
  </script>
   
  
<script type="text/javascript"> 
   //FIXED HEADER : MENU CATEGORIAS
   window.onscroll = function() {fixedHeader()};
   function fixedHeader(){
     var body_scrolltop    = document.body.scrollTop;
     var element_scrolltop = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
     if (body_scrolltop &gt; 350 || element_scrolltop &gt; 350) {
       $(".HeaderTopNav").hide();
       $(".header-row-1" ).hide();
       $(".header-row-2" ).hide();
       $(".HeaderTopNav").removeClass("visible-lg-block"); 
     }
     else{ 
       $(".HeaderTopNav" ).slideDown("slow");
       $(".header-row-1" ).slideDown( "slow" );
       $(".header-row-2" ).slideDown( "slow" );
       $(".HeaderTopNav").addClass("visible-lg-block");
     }
   }
</script> 
<script language="JavaScript">
function validar(string) {
    for (var i=0, output='', validos="/#@*+}]{[:!$%?ÃÂ¿ÃÂ¡&lt;&gt;ÃÂ°ÃÂº"; i&lt;string.length; i++)
       if (validos.indexOf(string.charAt(i)) == -1)
          output += string.charAt(i)
    return output;} 
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(function(){
            var showModal = new Boolean(false);
            var showModalShippingMethod = new Boolean(false);

            if(showModalShippingMethod == true &amp;&amp; showModal == true){
                $('#calendar-modal-content').modal('show');
            }
            $('input[name=select-method]').click(function(){
                showCalendar();
            });
        });
        function showCalendar(){
            var despatchMethod = $('input[name=select-method]:checked').val();
            var despatchCode = $('select.calendar-modal-select#'+despatchMethod).val();
            var data = {
                despatchCode : despatchCode,
                despatchMethod: despatchMethod
            };
            $.ajax({
                url: "/tottus/global/gadgets/ajaxCalendarModalDetail.jsp",
                method: "POST",
                data: data,
                dataType : "html",
                success: function(response){
                    $('.calendar-modal-detail').html(response);
                },
                complete: function(){
                    if(despatchMethod == "homeDelivery"){
                        $('.horarios-retiro').hide();
                        $('.horarios-despacho').show();
                        $('.title-collect').removeClass('green');
                        $('.title-delivery').addClass('green');
                    }else if(despatchMethod == "clickAndCollect"){
                        $('.horarios-retiro').show();
                        $('.horarios-despacho').hide();
                        $('.title-collect').addClass('green');
                        $('.title-delivery').removeClass('green');
                    }
                },
                error:function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError){
                    alert("failure "+thrownError);
                }
            });
        }
    </script>
